    <script type="text/javascript">
     function setChatCookie(cvalue, exdays) {
     var d = new Date();
     d.setTime(d.getTime() + (1*24*60*60*1000)); // 1 day
     var expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
     var id = Math.floor(Math.random() * Math.floor(999999999999));
     document.cookie = "cmc_chat_id=pega_chat_sess_"+id + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
 }
 function getChatCookie() {
     var cname = 'cmc_chat_id'
     var name = cname + "=";
     var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
     var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
     for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
         var c = ca[i];
         while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
             c = c.substring(1);
         }
         if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
             return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
         }
     }
     return "";
 }
 
 function InitChat(queue){
         window.fireflyAPI = window['fireflyChatAPI'] || {};
         window.fireflyAPI._log = window.fireflyAPI._log || function(){};
         window.fireflyChatAPI = {};
         fireflyChatAPI.token = "5a58cda481dd2d321a5aad90";
         fireflyChatAPI.assetHostUrl="https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.type = 'visitor';
         fireflyChatAPI.serverHostUrl = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.queue = queue;
         fireflyChatAPI.skipQueueSelection = true;
                 fireflyChatAPI.preChatAnswers = {"Account" : "no", "ContactId" : "no", "Product": "Website (DE)", "SessionId" : getChatCookie(), "Country" : "Germany", "PrefLanguage" : "DEU", "IPAddress": clientIP, "BrowserVersion": navigator.userAgent};
         var script = document.createElement("script");
         script.type = "text/javascript";
         script.src = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com/scripts/loaders/chatLoader_de.js";
         script.async = true;
         var firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
         firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(script, firstScript);
 }
 
 if ( getChatCookie() == '' ) {
     setChatCookie();
 }
 if( location.pathname != '/de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-at/') {
   var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
   var clientIP = '';
   request.open('GET', 'https://oaf.cmcmarkets.com/CmcApplicationFormsController/getPegaChatQueueREST?country=Germany&language=DEU', true);
   request.onload = function() {
     if (request.status >= 200 && request.status < 400) {
       response = JSON.parse(request.responseText);
           clientIP = response['client_ip_address'];
 queues = JSON.parse(response['queues']);
 queue = queues.shift();
           InitChat(queue );
     }
   };
   request.send();
 }
    </script>

     <div class="Section why-cmc-banner">
      <p class="h2 text-center">
       Warum CMC Markets?
      </p>
      <div class="container-fluid text-center">
       <div class="row why-cmc-items">
        <div class="col-md-6 col-lg-3 item-wrapper">
         <div class="why-cmc-item background-blue-dark">
          <img alt="Our focus is you" src="https://assets.cmcmarkets.com/fonts/value_money-white.svg?v=070916"/>
          <p class="h3">
           Der Kunde steht für uns im Mittelpunkt
          </p>
          <p>
           Unser Ziel ist es, Ihnen die beste Handelsplattform und den besten Service zu bieten

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function setChatCookie(cvalue, exdays) {
     var d = new Date();
     d.setTime(d.getTime() + (1*24*60*60*1000)); // 1 day
     var expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
     var id = Math.floor(Math.random() * Math.floor(999999999999));
     document.cookie = "cmc_chat_id=pega_chat_sess_"+id + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
 }
 function getChatCookie() {
     var cname = 'cmc_chat_id'
     var name = cname + "=";
     var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
     var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
     for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
         var c = ca[i];
         while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
             c = c.substring(1);
         }
         if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
             return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
         }
     }
     return "";
 }
 
 function InitChat(queue){
         window.fireflyAPI = window['fireflyChatAPI'] || {};
         window.fireflyAPI._log = window.fireflyAPI._log || function(){};
         window.fireflyChatAPI = {};
         fireflyChatAPI.token = "5a58cda481dd2d321a5aad90";
         fireflyChatAPI.assetHostUrl="https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.type = 'visitor';
         fireflyChatAPI.serverHostUrl = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.queue = queue;
         fireflyChatAPI.skipQueueSelection = true;
                 fireflyChatAPI.preChatAnswers = {"Account" : "no", "ContactId" : "no", "Product": "Website (DE)", "SessionId" : getChatCookie(), "Country" : "Germany", "PrefLanguage" : "DEU", "IPAddress": clientIP, "BrowserVersion": navigator.userAgent};
         var script = document.createElement("script");
         script.type = "text/javascript";
         script.src = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com/scripts/loaders/chatLoader_de.js";
         script.async = true;
         var firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
         firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(script, firstScript);
 }
 
 if ( getChatCookie() == '' ) {
     setChatCookie();
 }
 if( location.pathname != '/de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-at/') {
   var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
   var clientIP = '';
   request.open('GET', 'https://oaf.cmcmarkets.com/CmcApplicationFormsController/getPegaChatQueueREST?country=Germany&language=DEU', true);
   request.onload = function() {
     if (request.status >= 200 && request.status < 400) {
       response = JSON.parse(request.responseText);
           clientIP = response['client_ip_address'];
 queues = JSON.parse(response['queues']);
 queue = queues.shift();
           InitChat(queue );
     }
   };
   request.send();
 }
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function setChatCookie(cvalue, exdays) {
     var d = new Date();
     d.setTime(d.getTime() + (1*24*60*60*1000)); // 1 day
     var expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
     var id = Math.floor(Math.random() * Math.floor(999999999999));
     document.cookie = "cmc_chat_id=pega_chat_sess_"+id + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
 }
 function getChatCookie() {
     var cname = 'cmc_chat_id'
     var name = cname + "=";
     var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
     var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
     for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
         var c = ca[i];
         while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
             c = c.substring(1);
         }
         if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
             return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
         }
     }
     return "";
 }
 
 function InitChat(queue){
         window.fireflyAPI = window['fireflyChatAPI'] || {};
         window.fireflyAPI._log = window.fireflyAPI._log || function(){};
         window.fireflyChatAPI = {};
         fireflyChatAPI.token = "5a58cda481dd2d321a5aad90";
         fireflyChatAPI.assetHostUrl="https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.type = 'visitor';
         fireflyChatAPI.serverHostUrl = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.queue = queue;
         fireflyChatAPI.skipQueueSelection = true;
                 fireflyChatAPI.preChatAnswers = {"Account" : "no", "ContactId" : "no", "Product": "Website (DE)", "SessionId" : getChatCookie(), "Country" : "Germany", "PrefLanguage" : "DEU", "IPAddress": clientIP, "BrowserVersion": navigator.userAgent};
         var script = document.createElement("script");
         script.type = "text/javascript";
         script.src = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com/scripts/loaders/chatLoader_de.js";
         script.async = true;
         var firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
         firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(script, firstScript);
 }
 
 if ( getChatCookie() == '' ) {
     setChatCookie();
 }
 if( location.pathname != '/de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-at/') {
   var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
   var clientIP = '';
   request.open('GET', 'https://oaf.cmcmarkets.com/CmcApplicationFormsController/getPegaChatQueueREST?country=Germany&language=DEU', true);
   request.onload = function() {
     if (request.status >= 200 && request.status < 400) {
       response = JSON.parse(request.responseText);
           clientIP = response['client_ip_address'];
 queues = JSON.parse(response['queues']);
 queue = queues.shift();
           InitChat(queue );
     }
   };
   request.send();
 }
    </script>

     <div class="Section why-cmc-banner">
      <p class="h2 text-center">
       Warum CMC Markets?
      </p>
      <div class="container-fluid text-center">
       <div class="row why-cmc-items">
        <div class="col-md-6 col-lg-3 item-wrapper">

Sie sollten auch unsere Risikowarnungen für die jeweiligen Produkte lesen. Anlageerfolge in der Vergangenheit garantieren keine Erfolge in der Zukunft.

       CMC Markets UK Plc ist im Unternehmensregister der britischen Finanzmarktaufsichtsbehörde (Financial Conduct Authority) unter Registernummer 173730 registriert. Die Niederlassung Frankfurt am Main ist eine Zweigniederlassung im Sinne des § 53 b Abs. 1 KWG und wird von der FCA und der deutschen Finanzmarktaufsichtsbehörde (Bundesanstalt für Finanzdienstleistungsaufsicht, kurz BaFin) beaufsichtigt.

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function setChatCookie(cvalue, exdays) {
     var d = new Date();
     d.setTime(d.getTime() + (1*24*60*60*1000)); // 1 day
     var expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
     var id = Math.floor(Math.random() * Math.floor(999999999999));
     document.cookie = "cmc_chat_id=pega_chat_sess_"+id + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
 }
 function getChatCookie() {
     var cname = 'cmc_chat_id'
     var name = cname + "=";
     var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
     var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
     for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
         var c = ca[i];
         while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
             c = c.substring(1);
         }
         if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
             return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
         }
     }
     return "";
 }
 
 function InitChat(queue){
         window.fireflyAPI = window['fireflyChatAPI'] || {};
         window.fireflyAPI._log = window.fireflyAPI._log || function(){};
         window.fireflyChatAPI = {};
         fireflyChatAPI.token = "5a58cda481dd2d321a5aad90";
         fireflyChatAPI.assetHostUrl="https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.type = 'visitor';
         fireflyChatAPI.serverHostUrl = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.queue = queue;
         fireflyChatAPI.skipQueueSelection = true;
                 fireflyChatAPI.preChatAnswers = {"Account" : "no", "ContactId" : "no", "Product": "Website (DE)", "SessionId" : getChatCookie(), "Country" : "Germany", "PrefLanguage" : "DEU", "IPAddress": clientIP, "BrowserVersion": navigator.userAgent};
         var script = document.createElement("script");
         script.type = "text/javascript";
         script.src = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com/scripts/loaders/chatLoader_de.js";
         script.async = true;
         var firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
         firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(script, firstScript);
 }
 
 if ( getChatCookie() == '' ) {
     setChatCookie();
 }
 if( location.pathname != '/de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-at/') {
   var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
   var clientIP = '';
   request.open('GET', 'https://oaf.cmcmarkets.com/CmcApplicationFormsController/getPegaChatQueueREST?country=Germany&language=DEU', true);
   request.onload = function() {
     if (request.status >= 200 && request.status < 400) {
       response = JSON.parse(request.responseText);
           clientIP = response['client_ip_address'];
 queues = JSON.parse(response['queues']);
 queue = queues.shift();
           InitChat(queue );
     }
   };
   request.send();

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function setChatCookie(cvalue, exdays) {
     var d = new Date();
     d.setTime(d.getTime() + (1*24*60*60*1000)); // 1 day
     var expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
     var id = Math.floor(Math.random() * Math.floor(999999999999));
     document.cookie = "cmc_chat_id=pega_chat_sess_"+id + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
 }
 function getChatCookie() {
     var cname = 'cmc_chat_id'
     var name = cname + "=";
     var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
     var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
     for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
         var c = ca[i];
         while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
             c = c.substring(1);
         }
         if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
             return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
         }
     }
     return "";
 }
 
 function InitChat(queue){
         window.fireflyAPI = window['fireflyChatAPI'] || {};
         window.fireflyAPI._log = window.fireflyAPI._log || function(){};
         window.fireflyChatAPI = {};
         fireflyChatAPI.token = "5a58cda481dd2d321a5aad90";
         fireflyChatAPI.assetHostUrl="https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.type = 'visitor';
         fireflyChatAPI.serverHostUrl = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com";
         fireflyChatAPI.queue = queue;
         fireflyChatAPI.skipQueueSelection = true;
                 fireflyChatAPI.preChatAnswers = {"Account" : "no", "ContactId" : "no", "Product": "Website (DE)", "SessionId" : getChatCookie(), "Country" : "Germany", "PrefLanguage" : "DEU", "IPAddress": clientIP, "BrowserVersion": navigator.userAgent};
         var script = document.createElement("script");
         script.type = "text/javascript";
         script.src = "https://chat.cmcmarkets.com/scripts/loaders/chatLoader_de.js";
         script.async = true;
         var firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
         firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(script, firstScript);
 }
 
 if ( getChatCookie() == '' ) {
     setChatCookie();
 }
 if( location.pathname != '/de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-de/' &&  location.pathname != '/de-at/') {
   var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
   var clientIP = '';
   request.open('GET', 'https://oaf.cmcmarkets.com/CmcApplicationFormsController/getPegaChatQueueREST?country=Germany&language=DEU', true);
   request.onload = function() {
     if (request.status >= 200 && request.status < 400) {
       response = JSON.parse(request.responseText);
           clientIP = response['client_ip_address'];
 queues = JSON.parse(response['queues']);
 queue = queues.shift();
           InitChat(queue );
     }
   };
   request.send();
 }
    </script>
